Newport/Balboa Surface Temperature Data								
Newport Beach, CA   33°36.0'N   117°54.0'W								
Data are collected by Newport Beach Lifeguards with the City of Newport Beach.								
******* NOTE *******								
This data has been checked for key entry errors only.								
It has not been analyzed for overall quality.								
Data uncertainties are flagged with the following codes:								
0 = good data,								
1 = illegible entry,								
2 = data differs from other sources, ie. temperature vs. salinity records,								
3 = data uncertain,								
4 = leaky bottle,								
5 = SIO Pier Chlorophyll Program Data,								
6 = data collected at different location.								
Time flags indicate date or time uncertainties.								
Data flags indicate uncertainties with data.								
Time of sample collection available for 2003 - current								
data only and is converted to Pacific Standard Time (PST).								
Time of sample collection may be estimated for several measurements.								
==================================================================================								
***PLEASE CITE & REFERENCE THIS PROGRAM AS FOLLOWS***								
Shore Stations Program with current funding provided by the								
California Department of Boating and Waterways, Award# CA DWB 07-106-112								
Daily temperature and salinity measurements are collected by Newport Beach								
Lifeguards with the City of Newport Beach.								
Contact shorestation@ucsd.edu if you have questions.
